<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">

<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top;text-align:left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;5.02</span></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&#160;27, 2025, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc. <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;T-Mobile&#8221;)</span> appointed Srinivasan Gopalan as Chief Operating Officer (&#8220;COO&#8221;) of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> effective as of March&#160;1, 2025 (the &#8220;Effective Date&#8221;). </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s appointment as COO, on January&#160;27, 2025, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> entered into terms of employment (the &#8220;Agreement&#8221;) with Mr.&#160;Gopalan, which will become effective as of the Effective Date. Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s employment as COO under the Agreement will commence on the Effective Date and continue until terminated in accordance with the terms of the Agreement. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to the Agreement, Mr.&#160;Gopalan is entitled to (i)&#160;an annual base salary equal to $1,000,000; (ii) an annual short-term cash incentive targeted at no less than $2,000,000 (with a maximum award equal to 200% of target), payable based on the attainment of <span style="white-space:nowrap">pre-established&#160;performance</span> goals; (iii)&#160;employee benefits to the same extent and on the same terms as such benefits are provided generally by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> to its senior executives; (iv)&#160;company-paid or reimbursed tax preparation and financial planning services for calendar years 2025 and 2026 (capped at $50,000 per calendar year); (v) relocation assistance for costs associated with Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s relocation to the greater Bellevue, Washington area in accordance with the terms of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Relocation Policy, subject to <span style="white-space:nowrap">pro-rata</span> repayment in the event that Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s employment is terminated by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> for &#8220;cause&#8221; or by Mr.&#160;Gopalan without &#8220;good reason&#8221; (each as defined in the Agreement) within 12 months following the Effective Date; and (vi)&#160;company-paid or reimbursed first-class round-trip airfare for Mr.&#160;Gopalan and his spouse and children for 24 months following the Effective Date (capped at 32 round-trip flights in the aggregate and grossed up for applicable taxes). Mr.&#160;Gopalan is also eligible for a <span style="white-space:nowrap">one-time</span> cash payment of $2,000,000 (the <span style="white-space:nowrap">&#8220;Sign-On</span> Payment&#8221;), payable on or within 60 days following the Effective Date and subject to <span style="white-space:nowrap">pro-rata</span> repayment in the event that Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s employment is terminated by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> for &#8220;cause&#8221; or by Mr.&#160;Gopalan without &#8220;good reason&#8221; within 12 months following the Effective Date. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition, pursuant to the Agreement, Mr.&#160;Gopalan will be entitled to annual long-term incentive awards (&#8220;LTI awards&#8221;) with a target grant-date value of not less than $9,500,000. In connection with his commencement as COO, on or within 10 days following the Effective Date, Mr.&#160;Gopalan will be granted <span style="white-space:nowrap">a&#160;one-time&#160;award</span> of restricted stock units (&#8220;RSUs&#8221;) under the <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> 2023 Incentive Award Plan, with respect to a number of shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> common stock equal to (i)&#160;the estimated aggregate value of any phantom share awards granted to Mr.&#160;Gopalan prior to the Effective Date by Deutsche Telekom AG (&#8220;DT&#8221;) that are forfeited by Mr.&#160;Gopalan in connection with his commencement of employment with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> (such forfeited DT phantom share awards, the &#8220;Prior DT Awards&#8221;), based on the average closing price of an ordinary share of DT over the 30 <span style="white-space:nowrap">calendar-day</span> period ending five business days before (and the expected future performance of such Prior DT Awards as of) February&#160;28, 2025, divided by (ii)&#160;the average closing price of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> common stock over the 30 <span style="white-space:nowrap">calendar-day</span> period ending five business days before the grant date. A percentage of the RSUs subject to the award will vest on each of March&#160;1, 2026, March&#160;1, 2027, March&#160;1, 2028 and March&#160;1, 2029 (with the percentage of RSUs eligible to vest on each such date determined based on the percentage of phantom shares subject to the Prior DT Awards scheduled to vest during the same calendar year), subject to Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s continued employment with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> through the applicable vesting date (except as otherwise described below or provided in the applicable award agreement). </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the Agreement, Mr.&#160;Gopalan is also entitled to receive a cash payment (each, a &#8220;Match Payment&#8221;) on or within 60 days following each of May&#160;27, 2025, May&#160;18, 2026, May&#160;13, 2027 and May&#160;18, 2028 (each, a &#8220;Match Date&#8221;). The amount of each Match Payment will equal (i)&#160;the average closing price of an ordinary share of DT over the 30 <span style="white-space:nowrap">calendar-day</span> period ending five business days before the applicable Match Date, multiplied by (ii)&#160;the number of ordinary shares of DT released to Mr.&#160;Gopalan on such Match Date, subject to Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s continued employment with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> through the applicable payment date (except as otherwise described below). </p>
</div></div>

 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Agreement further provides that if Mr.&#160;Gopalan&#8217;s employment is terminated due to his death or disability, he will be entitled to receive the following: </p> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">

<td style="width:2%;vertical-align:top;text-align:left">&#8226;</td>
<td style="width:1%;vertical-align:top">&#160;</td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;text-align:left">any Prior Year STI; </p></td></tr></table> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">

<td style="width:1%;vertical-align:top">&#160;</td>

A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information contained in Item 7.01, including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall it be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.1
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE" STYLE="line-height:Normal">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US Appoints Srinivasan Gopalan as New Chief Operating Officer </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">New leader joins existing management team to continue growth and expansion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US business into
the next era </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">BELLEVUE, Wash. &#151; January&nbsp;27, 2025 &#151; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) today announced
the appointment of Srinivasan </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gopalan as its new Chief Operating Officer (COO). Mr.&nbsp;Gopalan will join
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US in his new role on March&nbsp;1, 2025, reporting directly to CEO Mike Sievert, and will lead the company&#146;s technology initiatives and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">go-to-market</FONT></FONT> operations across both Consumer and Business groups. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gopalan has served as a member of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> Board of Directors for nearly four years, with his most recent term beginning in 2022. His work as a member of the Board of Directors, along with his work on two important committees, has made a
lasting impact at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gopalan has extensive global leadership experience in technology, telecommunications,
and business operations. He has held senior leadership positions at organizations like Bharti Airtel in India, CapitalOne in the UK, Vodafone, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> UK where he contributed to the joint venture with Orange,
and various roles at Deutsche Telekom, including having served as the Managing Director of Telekom Deutschland GmbH, leading all operations and guiding DT&#146;s biggest operating country through a strategic digital transformation and market-leading
growth. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">He has successfully driven operational excellence, digital transformation, and customer-centric strategies, with a proven track record of
overseeing large-scale technology initiatives and leading <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">go-to-market</FONT></FONT> efforts that delivered growth and innovation. His combination of strategic vision, operational
rigor, and market-focused leadership makes him a tremendous choice to drive <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> continued success across Consumer and Business markets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I am so pleased to welcome Srini to this world-leading management team after working with him for years on our Board of Directors. I know from personal
experience that his deep understanding of technology, operations and our business makes him the ideal leader to take on the role of Chief Operating Officer,&#148; said Mike Sievert, CEO of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US.
&#147;As we execute on the multi-year business and technology transformation plan that we laid out at our Capital Markets Day, having Srini join our team couldn&#146;t be better timed, as he will leverage his experience and track record of leading
through significant transformations &#150; as a further accelerant to a plan that already has a lot of momentum behind it.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As COO, Gopalan will
focus on creating even better experiences for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> customers with an emphasis on technology work-streams that drive <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> towards its goal of being a data
informed, AI enabled, digital first company; and the integrated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">go-to-market</FONT></FONT> strategies that will make it a reality for customers and fuel
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> unique growth strategy. Expanding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> multi-year lead in network through advanced 5G solutions and driving thought leadership on the next
generation mobile network standards will also be a key area of focus. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I&#146;ve worked with Mike and this entire management team for many years as a board member, and
I&#146;m looking forward to joining management in this leadership role to build on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> momentum,&#148; said Mr.&nbsp;Gopalan. &#147;This is an important time for the company, the most exciting
chapter yet - and I look forward to jumping in to help drive the ongoing transformation in the Consumer and Business areas and to orchestrate the delivery of technology solutions and value.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The existing Senior Leadership Team will continue in their roles, and Jon Freier, President of the Consumer Group; Callie Field, President of the Business
Group; Nestor Cano, EVP Transformation and Chief Information and Digital Officer; and Ulf Ewaldsson, President of Technology will all report directly to Gopalan upon his arrival, which is expected to be March&nbsp;1, 2025.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) is America&#146;s supercharged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier,</FONT> delivering an advanced 4G LTE and transformative nationwide 5G network that will offer reliable
connectivity for all. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> customers benefit from its unmatched combination of value and quality, unwavering obsession with offering them the best possible service experience and undisputable drive
for disruption that creates competition and innovation in wireless and beyond. Based in Bellevue, Wash., <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> provides services through its subsidiaries and operates its flagship brands, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Metro by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Mint Mobile. For more information please visit:&nbsp;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://www.t-mobile.com</FONT></U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. Media Relations</B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">MediaRelations@t-mobile.com</FONT></U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Investor Relations Contact</B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">investor.relations@t-mobile.com</FONT></U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://investor.t-mobile.com</FONT></U></P>
